    SELECT p."Id", p."CategoryId", p."CreatedAt", p."Description", p."Name", p."Status", p."VendorId", v."Id" AS "Id0", v."ApprovedAt", v."Description" AS "Description0", v."GSTNumber", v."IsActive", v."LogoUrl", v."PANNumber", v."Status" AS "Status0", v."StoreEmail", v."StoreName", v."UserId", c."Id" AS "Id1", c."Name" AS "Name0", c."ParentId", c."isActive" AS "isActive0", c.slug
    FROM products AS p
    INNER JOIN vendors AS v ON p."VendorId" = v."Id"
    INNER JOIN categories AS c ON p."CategoryId" = c."Id"
    WHERE p."Id" = @id
    LIMIT 1
) AS s
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p0."Id", p0."AvailableValues", p0."IsActive", p0."IsDefault", p0."Price", p0."ProductId", p0."ReservedStockQty", p0."StockQty", p1."Id" AS "Id0", p1."ImageOrder", p1."ImageUrl", p1."VariantId"
    FROM product_variants AS p0
    LEFT JOIN product_images AS p1 ON p0."Id" = p1."VariantId"
    WHERE p0."IsActive"
) AS s0 ON s."Id" = s0."ProductId"
ORDER BY s."Id", s."Id0", s."Id1", s0."Id", s0."ImageOrder"

) AS s0 ON s."Id" = s0."ShipmentId"

    FROM order_items AS o
